function getID(id) {
    return document.getElementById(id);
}
function random(min, max) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min + 1)) + min;
}
function toRad(angle) {
    return angle * (Math.PI / 180);
}
let latency = 0;
const startTime = performance.now();

fetch(location.href)
    .then(response => {
    const endTime = performance.now();
    latency = Math.floor(endTime - startTime);
    // console.log(100/latency, latency)
})
getID("loadingText").innerText = "0%";

function setLoadText(text, time, i){
    setTimeout(()=>{
        if(i < (latency - 1)){
            getID("loadingText").innerText = Math.floor(text)+"%";
        }else{
            getID("loadingText").innerText = "100%";
        }
    },time);
}
let load = 0;
let loadText = setInterval(()=>{
    if(latency !=0){
        clearInterval(loadText)
        for(let i = 0; i < latency;i++){
            let time = (100/latency);
            load+=time
            console.log(load)
            setLoadText(load,latency*i, i)
        }
    }
});

let AFK = {
    time:  Date.now(),
    lock: false,
    size: [],
    mousedown: false
}
window.addEventListener('mousedown', function (e) {
    if(!AFK.lock){
        AFK.time = Date.now();
    }
});
window.addEventListener('mousemove', function (e) {
    if(!AFK.lock){
        AFK.time = Date.now();
    }
});
window.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
    if(!AFK.lock){
        AFK.time = Date.now();
    }
});

getID("AFK").addEventListener('mousedown', function (e) {
    AFK.size = [];
    AFK.mousedown = true;
    let StartY = e.clientY;
    let prevY = e.clientY;
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', mousemove);
    window.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseup);
    function mousemove(e) {
        let newY = prevY - e.clientY;
        const rect = getID("AFK").getBoundingClientRect();
        getID("AFK").style.top = rect.top - newY + 'px';
        prevY = e.clientY;
        if((StartY - e.clientY) > window.innerHeight/10){
            if(newY > 0){
                AFK.size.push(newY);
            }
            AFK.time = Date.now();
            AFK.lock = true;
        }
    }
    function mouseup() {
        AFK.mousedown = false;
        window.removeEventListener('mousemove', mousemove);
        window.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseup);
    }
});

            console.warn("Socket connection error:", n),
                t(n)
        }
    },
    send: function(e) {
        const t = Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1)
        , i = Ll.encode([e, t]);
        this.socket && this.socket.send(i)
    },
    socketReady: function() {
        return this.socket && this.connected
    },
    close: function() {
        this.socket && this.socket.close(),
            this.socket = null,
            this.connected = !1
    }
};

var Vr = Math.abs;
const ql = Math.sqrt;
const Wl = Math.atan2
, Qi = Math.PI
, Xl = function(e, t) {
    return Math.floor(Math.random() * (t - e + 1)) + e
}
, Gl = function(e, t) {
    return Math.random() * (t - e + 1) + e
}
, Yl = function(e, t, i) {
    return e + (t - e) * i
}
, $l = function(e, t) {
    return e > 0 ? e = Math.max(0, e - t) : e < 0 && (e = Math.min(0, e + t)),
        e
}
, Kl = function(e, t, i, s) {
    return ql((i -= e) * i + (s -= t) * s)
}
, Jl = function(e, t, i, s) {
    return Wl(t - s, e - i)
}
, Ql = function(e, t) {
    const i = Vr(t - e) % (Qi * 2);
    return i > Qi ? Qi * 2 - i : i
}
, Zl = function(e) {
    return typeof e == "number" && !isNaN(e) && isFinite(e)
}
, jl = function(e) {
    return e && typeof e == "string"
}
, ec = function(e) {
    return e > 999 ? (e / 1e3).toFixed(1) + "k" : e
}
, tc = function(e) {
    return e.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + e.slice(1)
}
, ic = function(e, t) {
    return e ? parseFloat(e.toFixed(t)) : 0
}
, nc = function(e, t) {
    return parseFloat(t.points) - parseFloat(e.points)
}
, sc = function(e, t, i, s, n, r, o, l) {
    let c = n
    , a = o;
    if (n > o && (c = o,
                  a = n),
        a > i && (a = i),
        c < e && (c = e),
        c > a)
        return !1;
    let u = r
    , p = l;
    const h = o - n;
    if (Math.abs(h) > 1e-7) {
        const m = (l - r) / h
        , w = r - m * n;
        u = m * c + w,
            p = m * a + w
    }
    if (u > p) {
        const m = p;
        p = u,
            u = m
    }
    return p > s && (p = s),
        u < t && (u = t),
        !(u > p)
}
, Ur = function(e, t, i) {
    const s = e.getBoundingClientRect()
    , n = s.left + window.scrollX
    , r = s.top + window.scrollY
    , o = s.width
    , l = s.height
    , c = t > n && t < n + o
    , a = i > r && i < r + l;
    return c && a
}
, li = function(e) {
    const t = e.changedTouches[0];
    e.screenX = t.screenX,
        e.screenY = t.screenY,
        e.clientX = t.clientX,
        e.clientY = t.clientY,
        e.pageX = t.pageX,
        e.pageY = t.pageY
}
, Lr = function(e, t) {
    const i = !t;
    let s = !1;
    const n = !1;
    e.addEventListener("touchstart", Be(r), n),
        e.addEventListener("touchmove", Be(o), n),
        e.addEventListener("touchend", Be(l), n),
        e.addEventListener("touchcancel", Be(l), n),
        e.addEventListener("touchleave", Be(l), n);
    function r(c) {
        li(c),
            window.setUsingTouch(!0),
            i && (c.preventDefault(),
                  c.stopPropagation()),
            e.onmouseover && e.onmouseover(c),
            s = !0
    }
    function o(c) {
        li(c),
            window.setUsingTouch(!0),
            i && (c.preventDefault(),
                  c.stopPropagation()),
            Ur(e, c.pageX, c.pageY) ? s || (e.onmouseover && e.onmouseover(c),
                                            s = !0) : s && (e.onmouseout && e.onmouseout(c),
                                                            s = !1)
    }
    function l(c) {
        li(c),
            window.setUsingTouch(!0),
            i && (c.preventDefault(),
                  c.stopPropagation()),
            s && (e.onclick && e.onclick(c),
                  e.onmouseout && e.onmouseout(c),
                  s = !1)
    }
}
, rc = function(e) {
    for (; e.hasChildNodes(); )
        e.removeChild(e.lastChild)
}
, oc = function(e) {
    const t = document.createElement(e.tag || "div");
    function i(s, n) {
        e[s] && (t[n] = e[s])
    }
    i("text", "textContent"),
        i("html", "innerHTML"),
        i("class", "className");
    for (const s in e) {
        switch (s) {
            case "tag":
            case "text":
            case "html":
            case "class":
            case "style":
            case "hookTouch":
            case "parent":
            case "children":
                continue
        }
        t[s] = e[s]
    }
    if (t.onclick && (t.onclick = Be(t.onclick)),
        t.onmouseover && (t.onmouseover = Be(t.onmouseover)),
        t.onmouseout && (t.onmouseout = Be(t.onmouseout)),
        e.style && (t.style.cssText = e.style),
        e.hookTouch && Lr(t),
        e.parent && e.parent.appendChild(t),
        e.children)
        for (let s = 0; s < e.children.length; s++)
            t.appendChild(e.children[s]);
    return t
}
, Nr = function(e) {
    return e && typeof e.isTrusted == "boolean" ? e.isTrusted : !0
}
, Be = function(e) {
    return function(t) {
        t && t instanceof Event && Nr(t) && e(t)
    }
}
, ac = function(e) {
    let t = "";
    const i = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789";
    for (let s = 0; s < e; s++)
        t += i.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * i.length));
    return t
}
, lc = function(e, t) {
    let i = 0;
    for (let s = 0; s < e.length; s++)
        e[s] === t && i++;
    return i
}
, C = {
    randInt: Xl,

, cc = function() {
    this.init = function(e, t, i, s, n, r, o) {
        this.x = e,
            this.y = t,
            this.color = o,
            this.scale = i,
            this.startScale = this.scale,
            this.maxScale = i * 1.5,
            this.scaleSpeed = .7,
            this.speed = s,
            this.life = n,
            this.text = r
    }
        ,
        this.update = function(e) {
        this.life && (this.life -= e,
                      this.y -= this.speed * e,
                      this.scale += this.scaleSpeed * e,
                      this.scale >= this.maxScale ? (this.scale = this.maxScale,
                                                     this.scaleSpeed *= -1) : this.scale <= this.startScale && (this.scale = this.startScale,
                                                                                                                this.scaleSpeed = 0),
                      this.life <= 0 && (this.life = 0))
    }
        ,
        this.render = function(e, t, i) {
        e.fillStyle = this.color,
            e.font = this.scale + "px Hammersmith One",
            e.fillText(this.text, this.x - t, this.y - i)
    }
}
, hc = function() {
    this.texts = [],
        this.update = function(e, t, i, s) {

            t.textAlign = "center";

                                   this.texts[n].render(t, i, s))
    }
        ,
        this.showText = function(e, t, i, s, n, r, o) {
        let l;
        for (let c = 0; c < this.texts.length; ++c)
            if (!this.texts[c].life) {
                l = this.texts[c];
                break
            }
        l || (l = new cc,
              this.texts.push(l)),
            l.init(e, t, i, s, n, r, o)
    }
}
, fc = function(e, t) {

, Cs = Math.floor
, As = Math.abs
, Ot = Math.cos
, Rt = Math.sin
, uc = Math.sqrt;
function dc(e, t, i, s, n, r) {
    this.objects = t,
        this.grids = {},
        this.updateObjects = [];
    let o, l;
    const c = s.mapScale / s.colGrid;
    this.setObjectGrids = function(h) {
        const m = Math.min(s.mapScale, Math.max(0, h.x))
        , w = Math.min(s.mapScale, Math.max(0, h.y));
        for (let v = 0; v < s.colGrid; ++v) {
            o = v * c;
            for (let x = 0; x < s.colGrid; ++x)
                l = x * c,
                    m + h.scale >= o && m - h.scale <= o + c && w + h.scale >= l && w - h.scale <= l + c && (this.grids[v + "_" + x] || (this.grids[v + "_" + x] = []),
                                                                                                             this.grids[v + "_" + x].push(h),
                                                                                                             h.gridLocations.push(v + "_" + x))
        }
    }
        ,
        this.removeObjGrid = function(h) {
        let m;
        for (let w = 0; w < h.gridLocations.length; ++w)
            m = this.grids[h.gridLocations[w]].indexOf(h),
                m >= 0 && this.grids[h.gridLocations[w]].splice(m, 1)
    }
        ,
        this.disableObj = function(h) {
        if (h.active = !1,
            r) {
            h.owner && h.pps && (h.owner.pps -= h.pps),
                this.removeObjGrid(h);
            const m = this.updateObjects.indexOf(h);
            m >= 0 && this.updateObjects.splice(m, 1)
        }
    }
        ,
        this.hitObj = function(h, m) {
        for (let w = 0; w < n.length; ++w)
            n[w].active && (h.sentTo[n[w].id] && (h.active ? n[w].canSee(h) && r.send(n[w].id, "L", i.fixTo(m, 1), h.sid) : r.send(n[w].id, "Q", h.sid)),
                            !h.active && h.owner == n[w] && n[w].changeItemCount(h.group.id, -1))
    }
    ;
    const a = [];
    let u;
    this.getGridArrays = function(h, m, w) {
        o = Cs(h / c),
            l = Cs(m / c),
            a.length = 0;
        try {
            this.grids[o + "_" + l] && a.push(this.grids[o + "_" + l]),
                h + w >= (o + 1) * c && (u = this.grids[o + 1 + "_" + l],
                                         u && a.push(u),
                                         l && m - w <= l * c ? (u = this.grids[o + 1 + "_" + (l - 1)],
                                                                u && a.push(u)) : m + w >= (l + 1) * c && (u = this.grids[o + 1 + "_" + (l + 1)],
                                                                                                           u && a.push(u))),
                o && h - w <= o * c && (u = this.grids[o - 1 + "_" + l],
                                        u && a.push(u),
                                        l && m - w <= l * c ? (u = this.grids[o - 1 + "_" + (l - 1)],
                                                               u && a.push(u)) : m + w >= (l + 1) * c && (u = this.grids[o - 1 + "_" + (l + 1)],
                                                                                                          u && a.push(u))),
                m + w >= (l + 1) * c && (u = this.grids[o + "_" + (l + 1)],
                                         u && a.push(u)),
                l && m - w <= l * c && (u = this.grids[o + "_" + (l - 1)],
                                        u && a.push(u))
        } catch {}
        return a
    }
    ;
    let p;
    this.add = function(h, m, w, v, x, A, k, T, O) {
        p = null;
        for (var V = 0; V < t.length; ++V)
            if (t[V].sid == h) {
                p = t[V];
                break
            }
        if (!p) {
            for (var V = 0; V < t.length; ++V)
                if (!t[V].active) {
                    p = t[V];
                    break
                }
        }
        p || (p = new e(h),
              t.push(p)),
            T && (p.sid = h),
            p.init(m, w, v, x, A, k, O),
            r && (this.setObjectGrids(p),
                  p.doUpdate && this.updateObjects.push(p))
    }
        ,
        this.disableBySid = function(h) {
        for (let m = 0; m < t.length; ++m)
            if (t[m].sid == h) {
                this.disableObj(t[m]);
                break
            }
    }
        ,
        this.removeAllItems = function(h, m) {
        for (let w = 0; w < t.length; ++w)
            t[w].active && t[w].owner && t[w].owner.sid == h && this.disableObj(t[w]);
        m && m.broadcast("R", h)
    }
        ,
        this.fetchSpawnObj = function(h) {
        let m = null;
        for (let w = 0; w < t.length; ++w)
            if (p = t[w],
                p.active && p.owner && p.owner.sid == h && p.spawnPoint) {
                m = [p.x, p.y],
                    this.disableObj(p),
                    r.broadcast("Q", p.sid),
                    p.owner && p.owner.changeItemCount(p.group.id, -1);
                break
            }
        return m
    }
        ,
        this.checkItemLocation = function(h, m, w, v, x, A, k) {
        for (let T = 0; T < t.length; ++T) {
            const O = t[T].blocker ? t[T].blocker : t[T].getScale(v, t[T].isItem);
            if (t[T].active && i.getDistance(h, m, t[T].x, t[T].y) < w + O)
                return !1
        }
        return !(!A && x != 18 && m >= s.mapScale / 2 - s.riverWidth / 2 && m <= s.mapScale / 2 + s.riverWidth / 2)
    }
        ,
        this.addProjectile = function(h, m, w, v, x) {
        const A = items.projectiles[x];
        let k;
        for (let T = 0; T < projectiles.length; ++T)
            if (!projectiles[T].active) {
                k = projectiles[T];
                break
            }
        k || (k = new Projectile(n,i),
              projectiles.push(k)),
            k.init(x, h, m, w, A.speed, v, A.scale)
    }
        ,
        this.checkCollision = function(h, m, w) {
        w = w || 1;
        const v = h.x - m.x
        , x = h.y - m.y;
        let A = h.scale + m.scale;
        if (As(v) <= A || As(x) <= A) {
            A = h.scale + (m.getScale ? m.getScale() : m.scale);
            let k = uc(v * v + x * x) - A;
            if (k <= 0) {
                if (m.ignoreCollision)
                    m.trap && !h.noTrap && m.owner != h && !(m.owner && m.owner.team && m.owner.team == h.team) ? (h.lockMove = !0,
                                                                                                                   m.hideFromEnemy = !1) : m.boostSpeed ? (h.xVel += w * m.boostSpeed * (m.weightM || 1) * Ot(m.dir),
                    h.yVel += w * m.boostSpeed * (m.weightM || 1) * Rt(m.dir)) : m.healCol ? h.healCol = m.healCol : m.teleport && (h.x = i.randInt(0, s.mapScale),
                                                                                                                                    h.y = i.randInt(0, s.mapScale));
                else {
                    const T = i.getDirection(h.x, h.y, m.x, m.y);
                    if (i.getDistance(h.x, h.y, m.x, m.y),
                        m.isPlayer ? (k = k * -1 / 2,
                                      h.x += k * Ot(T),
                                      h.y += k * Rt(T),
                                      m.x -= k * Ot(T),
                                      m.y -= k * Rt(T)) : (h.x = m.x + A * Ot(T),
                                                           h.y = m.y + A * Rt(T),
                                                           h.xVel *= .75,
                                                           h.yVel *= .75),
                        m.dmg && m.owner != h && !(m.owner && m.owner.team && m.owner.team == h.team)) {
                        h.changeHealth(-m.dmg, m.owner, m);
                        const O = 1.5 * (m.weightM || 1);
                        h.xVel += O * Ot(T),
                            h.yVel += O * Rt(T),
                            m.pDmg && !(h.skin && h.skin.poisonRes) && (h.dmgOverTime.dmg = m.pDmg,
                                                                        h.dmgOverTime.time = 5,
                                                                        h.dmgOverTime.doer = m.owner),
                            h.colDmg && m.health && (m.changeHealth(-h.colDmg) && this.disableObj(m),
                                                     this.hitObj(m, i.getDirection(h.x, h.y, m.x, m.y)))
                    }
                }
                return m.zIndex > h.zIndex && (h.zIndex = m.zIndex),
                    !0
            }
        }
        return !1
    }
}

}

        weightM: .45,
        speed: .00115,

        scale: 88,
        viewRange: 1440,

        drop: ["food", 400],
        minSpawnRange: .85,
        maxSpawnRange: .9
    }, {
        id: 11,
        name: "💀Bully",
        src: "bull_1",
        hostile: !0,
        fixedSpawn: !0,
        dontRun: !0,
        hitScare: 50,
        dmg: 20,
        killScore: 5e3,
        health: 5e3,
        spawnDelay: 1e5,
        weightM: .45,
        speed: .00115,
        turnSpeed: .0025,
        scale: 94,
        viewRange: 1440,
        chargePlayer: !0,
        drop: ["food", 800],
        minSpawnRange: .85,
        maxSpawnRange: .9
    }],
        this.spawn = function(a, u, p, h) {
        if (!this.aiTypes[h])
            return console.error("missing ai type", h),
                this.spawn(a, u, p, 0);
        let m;
        for (let w = 0; w < e.length; ++w)
            if (!e[w].active) {
                m = e[w];
                break
            }
        return m || (m = new t(e.length,n,i,s,o,r,l,c),
                     e.push(m)),
            m.init(a, u, p, h, this.aiTypes[h]),
            m
    }
}
const st = Math.PI * 2
, Zi = 0;
function gc(e, t, i, s, n, r, o, l) {
    this.sid = e,
        this.isAI = !0,
        this.nameIndex = n.randInt(0, r.cowNames.length - 1),
        this.init = function(p, h, m, w, v) {
        this.x = p,
            this.y = h,
            this.startX = v.fixedSpawn ? p : null,
            this.startY = v.fixedSpawn ? h : null,
            this.xVel = 0,
            this.yVel = 0,
            this.zIndex = 0,
            this.dir = m,
            this.dirPlus = 0,
            this.index = w,
            this.src = v.src,
            v.name && (this.name = v.name),
            (this.name || "").startsWith("💀") && (this.isVolcanoAi = !0),
            this.weightM = v.weightM,
            this.speed = v.speed,
            this.killScore = v.killScore,
            this.turnSpeed = v.turnSpeed,
            this.scale = v.scale,
            this.maxHealth = v.health,
            this.leapForce = v.leapForce,
            this.health = this.maxHealth,
            this.chargePlayer = v.chargePlayer,
            this.viewRange = v.viewRange,
            this.drop = v.drop,
            this.dmg = v.dmg,
            this.hostile = v.hostile,
            this.dontRun = v.dontRun,
            this.hitRange = v.hitRange,
            this.hitDelay = v.hitDelay,
            this.hitScare = v.hitScare,
            this.spriteMlt = v.spriteMlt,
            this.nameScale = v.nameScale,
            this.colDmg = v.colDmg,
            this.noTrap = v.noTrap,
            this.spawnDelay = v.spawnDelay,
            this.minSpawnRange = v.minSpawnRange,
            this.maxSpawnRange = v.maxSpawnRange,
            this.hitWait = 0,
            this.waitCount = 1e3,
            this.moveCount = 0,
            this.targetDir = 0,
            this.active = !0,
            this.alive = !0,
            this.runFrom = null,
            this.chargeTarget = null,
            this.dmgOverTime = {}
    }
        ,
        this.getVolcanoAggression = function() {
        const p = n.getDistance(this.x, this.y, r.volcanoLocationX, r.volcanoLocationY)
        , h = p > r.volcanoAggressionRadius ? 0 : r.volcanoAggressionRadius - p;
        return 1 + r.volcanoAggressionPercentage * (1 - h / r.volcanoAggressionRadius)
    }
    ;
    let c = 0;
    this.update = function(p) {
        if (this.active) {
            if (this.spawnCounter) {
                if (this.spawnCounter -= p * (1 + 0) * this.getVolcanoAggression(),
                    this.spawnCounter <= 0)
                    if (this.spawnCounter = 0,
                        this.minSpawnRange || this.maxSpawnRange) {
                        const U = r.mapScale * this.minSpawnRange
                        , L = r.mapScale * this.maxSpawnRange;
                        this.x = n.randInt(U, L),
                            this.y = n.randInt(U, L)
                    } else
                        this.x = this.startX || n.randInt(0, r.mapScale),
                            this.y = this.startY || n.randInt(0, r.mapScale);
                return
            }
            c -= p,
                c <= 0 && (this.dmgOverTime.dmg && (this.changeHealth(-this.dmgOverTime.dmg, this.dmgOverTime.doer),
                                                    this.dmgOverTime.time -= 1,
                                                    this.dmgOverTime.time <= 0 && (this.dmgOverTime.dmg = 0)),
                           c = 1e3);
            let k = !1
            , T = 1;
            if (!this.zIndex && !this.lockMove && this.y >= r.mapScale / 2 - r.riverWidth / 2 && this.y <= r.mapScale / 2 + r.riverWidth / 2 && (T = .33,
                                                                                                                                                 this.xVel += r.waterCurrent * p),
                this.lockMove)
                this.xVel = 0,
                    this.yVel = 0;
            else if (this.waitCount > 0) {
                if (this.waitCount -= p,
                    this.waitCount <= 0)
                    if (this.chargePlayer) {
                        let U, L, _;
                        for (var h = 0; h < i.length; ++h)
                            i[h].alive && !(i[h].skin && i[h].skin.bullRepel) && (_ = n.getDistance(this.x, this.y, i[h].x, i[h].y),
                                                                                  _ <= this.viewRange && (!U || _ < L) && (L = _,
                                                                                                                           U = i[h]));
                        U ? (this.chargeTarget = U,
                             this.moveCount = n.randInt(8e3, 12e3)) : (this.moveCount = n.randInt(1e3, 2e3),
                                                                       this.targetDir = n.randFloat(-Math.PI, Math.PI))
                    } else
                        this.moveCount = n.randInt(4e3, 1e4),
                            this.targetDir = n.randFloat(-Math.PI, Math.PI)
            } else if (this.moveCount > 0) {
                var m = this.speed * T * (1 + r.MAX_SPEED * Zi) * this.getVolcanoAggression();
                if (this.runFrom && this.runFrom.active && !(this.runFrom.isPlayer && !this.runFrom.alive) ? (this.targetDir = n.getDirection(this.x, this.y, this.runFrom.x, this.runFrom.y),
                                                                                                              m *= 1.42) : this.chargeTarget && this.chargeTarget.alive && (this.targetDir = n.getDirection(this.chargeTarget.x, this.chargeTarget.y, this.x, this.y),
                m *= 1.75,
                k = !0),
                    this.hitWait && (m *= .3),
                    this.dir != this.targetDir) {
                    this.dir %= st;
                    const U = (this.dir - this.targetDir + st) % st
                    , L = Math.min(Math.abs(U - st), U, this.turnSpeed * p)
                    , _ = U - Math.PI >= 0 ? 1 : -1;
                    this.dir += _ * L + st
                }
                this.dir %= st,
                    this.xVel += m * p * Math.cos(this.dir),
                    this.yVel += m * p * Math.sin(this.dir),
                    this.moveCount -= p,
                    this.moveCount <= 0 && (this.runFrom = null,
                                            this.chargeTarget = null,
                                            this.waitCount = this.hostile ? 1500 : n.randInt(1500, 6e3))
            }
            this.zIndex = 0,
                this.lockMove = !1;
            var w;
            const O = n.getDistance(0, 0, this.xVel * p, this.yVel * p)
            , V = Math.min(4, Math.max(1, Math.round(O / 40)))
            , N = 1 / V;
            for (var h = 0; h < V; ++h) {
                this.xVel && (this.x += this.xVel * p * N),
                    this.yVel && (this.y += this.yVel * p * N),
                    w = t.getGridArrays(this.x, this.y, this.scale);
                for (var v = 0; v < w.length; ++v)
                    for (let L = 0; L < w[v].length; ++L)
                        w[v][L].active && t.checkCollision(this, w[v][L], N)
            }
            let W = !1;
            if (this.hitWait > 0 && (this.hitWait -= p,
                                     this.hitWait <= 0)) {
                W = !0,
                    this.hitWait = 0,
                    this.leapForce && !n.randInt(0, 2) && (this.xVel += this.leapForce * Math.cos(this.dir),
                                                           this.yVel += this.leapForce * Math.sin(this.dir));
                var w = t.getGridArrays(this.x, this.y, this.hitRange), x, A;
                for (let L = 0; L < w.length; ++L)
                    for (var v = 0; v < w[L].length; ++v)
                        x = w[L][v],
                            x.health && (A = n.getDistance(this.x, this.y, x.x, x.y),
                                         A < x.scale + this.hitRange && (x.changeHealth(-this.dmg * 5) && t.disableObj(x),
                                                                         t.hitObj(x, n.getDirection(this.x, this.y, x.x, x.y))));
                for (var v = 0; v < i.length; ++v)
                    i[v].canSee(this) && l.send(i[v].id, "J", this.sid)
            }
            if (k || W) {
                var x, A;
                let _;
                for (var h = 0; h < i.length; ++h)
                    x = i[h],
                        x && x.alive && (A = n.getDistance(this.x, this.y, x.x, x.y),
                                         this.hitRange ? !this.hitWait && A <= this.hitRange + x.scale && (W ? (_ = n.getDirection(x.x, x.y, this.x, this.y),
                                                                                                                x.changeHealth(-this.dmg * (1 + r.MAX_ATTACK * Zi) * this.getVolcanoAggression()),
                                                                                                                x.xVel += .6 * Math.cos(_),
                                                                                                                x.yVel += .6 * Math.sin(_),
                                                                                                                this.runFrom = null,
                                                                                                                this.chargeTarget = null,
                                                                                                                this.waitCount = 3e3,
                                                                                                                this.hitWait = n.randInt(0, 2) ? 0 : 600) : this.hitWait = this.hitDelay) : A <= this.scale + x.scale && (_ = n.getDirection(x.x, x.y, this.x, this.y),
                    x.changeHealth(-this.dmg * (1 + r.MAX_ATTACK * Zi) * this.getVolcanoAggression()),
                    x.xVel += .55 * Math.cos(_),
                    x.yVel += .55 * Math.sin(_)))
            }
            this.xVel && (this.xVel *= Math.pow(r.playerDecel, p)),
                this.yVel && (this.yVel *= Math.pow(r.playerDecel, p));
            const P = this.scale;
            this.x - P < 0 ? (this.x = P,
                              this.xVel = 0) : this.x + P > r.mapScale && (this.x = r.mapScale - P,
                                                                           this.xVel = 0),
                this.y - P < 0 ? (this.y = P,
                                  this.yVel = 0) : this.y + P > r.mapScale && (this.y = r.mapScale - P,
                                                                               this.yVel = 0),
                this.isVolcanoAi && (this.chargeTarget && (n.getDistance(this.chargeTarget.x, this.chargeTarget.y, r.volcanoLocationX, r.volcanoLocationY) || 0) > r.volcanoAggressionRadius && (this.chargeTarget = null),
                                     this.xVel && (this.x < r.volcanoLocationX - r.volcanoAggressionRadius ? (this.x = r.volcanoLocationX - r.volcanoAggressionRadius,
                                                                                                              this.xVel = 0) : this.x > r.volcanoLocationX + r.volcanoAggressionRadius && (this.x = r.volcanoLocationX + r.volcanoAggressionRadius,
            this.xVel = 0)),
                                     this.yVel && (this.y < r.volcanoLocationY - r.volcanoAggressionRadius ? (this.y = r.volcanoLocationY - r.volcanoAggressionRadius,
                                                                                                              this.yVel = 0) : this.y > r.volcanoLocationY + r.volcanoAggressionRadius && (this.y = r.volcanoLocationY + r.volcanoAggressionRadius,
            this.yVel = 0)))
        }
    }
        ,
        this.canSee = function(p) {
        if (!p || p.skin && p.skin.invisTimer && p.noMovTimer >= p.skin.invisTimer)
            return !1;
        const h = Math.abs(p.x - this.x) - p.scale
        , m = Math.abs(p.y - this.y) - p.scale;
        return h <= r.maxScreenWidth / 2 * 1.3 && m <= r.maxScreenHeight / 2 * 1.3
    }
    ;
    let a = 0
    , u = 0;
    this.animate = function(p) {
        this.animTime > 0 && (this.animTime -= p,
                              this.animTime <= 0 ? (this.animTime = 0,
                                                    this.dirPlus = 0,
                                                    a = 0,
                                                    u = 0) : u == 0 ? (a += p / (this.animSpeed * r.hitReturnRatio),
                                                                       this.dirPlus = n.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.min(1, a)),
                                                                       a >= 1 && (a = 1,
                                                                                  u = 1)) : (a -= p / (this.animSpeed * (1 - r.hitReturnRatio)),
                                                                                             this.dirPlus = n.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.max(0, a))))
    }
        ,
        this.startAnim = function() {
        this.animTime = this.animSpeed = 600,
            this.targetAngle = Math.PI * .8,
            a = 0,
            u = 0
    }
        ,
        this.changeHealth = function(p, h, m) {
        if (this.active && (this.health += p,
                            m && (this.hitScare && !n.randInt(0, this.hitScare) ? (this.runFrom = m,
                                                                                   this.waitCount = 0,
                                                                                   this.moveCount = 2e3) : this.hostile && this.chargePlayer && m.isPlayer ? (this.chargeTarget = m,
        this.waitCount = 0,
        this.moveCount = 8e3) : this.dontRun || (this.runFrom = m,
                                                 this.waitCount = 0,
                                                 this.moveCount = 2e3)),
                            p < 0 && this.hitRange && n.randInt(0, 1) && (this.hitWait = 500),
                            h && h.canSee(this) && p < 0 && l.send(h.id, "8", Math.round(this.x), Math.round(this.y), Math.round(-p), 1),
                            this.health <= 0)) {
            if (this.spawnDelay)
                this.spawnCounter = this.spawnDelay,
                    this.x = -1e6,
                    this.y = -1e6;
            else if (this.minSpawnRange || this.maxSpawnRange) {
                const w = r.mapScale * this.minSpawnRange
                , v = r.mapScale * this.maxSpawnRange;
                this.x = n.randInt(w, v),
                    this.y = n.randInt(w, v)
            } else
                this.x = this.startX || n.randInt(0, r.mapScale),
                    this.y = this.startY || n.randInt(0, r.mapScale);
            if (this.health = this.maxHealth,
                this.runFrom = null,
                h && (o(h, this.killScore),
                      this.drop))
                for (let w = 0; w < this.drop.length; )
                    h.addResource(r.resourceTypes.indexOf(this.drop[w]), this.drop[w + 1]),
                        w += 2
        }
    }
}
function yc(e) {
    this.sid = e,
        this.init = function(t, i, s, n, r, o, l) {
        o = o || {},
            this.sentTo = {},
            this.gridLocations = [],
            this.active = !0,
            this.doUpdate = o.doUpdate,
            this.x = t,
            this.y = i,
            this.dir = s,
            this.xWiggle = 0,
            this.yWiggle = 0,
            this.scale = n,
            this.type = r,
            this.id = o.id,
            this.owner = l,
            this.name = o.name,
            this.isItem = this.id != null,
            this.group = o.group,
            this.health = o.health,
            this.layer = 2,
            this.group != null ? this.layer = this.group.layer : this.type == 0 ? this.layer = 3 : this.type == 2 ? this.layer = 0 : this.type == 4 && (this.layer = -1),
            this.colDiv = o.colDiv || 1,
            this.blocker = o.blocker,
            this.ignoreCollision = o.ignoreCollision,
            this.dontGather = o.dontGather,
            this.hideFromEnemy = o.hideFromEnemy,
            this.friction = o.friction,
            this.projDmg = o.projDmg,
            this.dmg = o.dmg,
            this.pDmg = o.pDmg,
            this.pps = o.pps,
            this.zIndex = o.zIndex || 0,
            this.turnSpeed = o.turnSpeed,
            this.req = o.req,
            this.trap = o.trap,
            this.healCol = o.healCol,
            this.teleport = o.teleport,
            this.boostSpeed = o.boostSpeed,
            this.projectile = o.projectile,
            this.shootRange = o.shootRange,
            this.shootRate = o.shootRate,
            this.shootCount = this.shootRate,
            this.spawnPoint = o.spawnPoint
    }
        ,
        this.changeHealth = function(t, i) {
        return this.health += t,
            this.health <= 0
    }
        ,
        this.getScale = function(t, i) {
        return t = t || 1,
            this.scale * (this.isItem || this.type == 2 || this.type == 3 || this.type == 4 ? 1 : .6 * t) * (i ? 1 : this.colDiv)
    }
        ,
        this.visibleToPlayer = function(t) {
        return !this.hideFromEnemy || this.owner && (this.owner == t || this.owner.team && t.team == this.owner.team)
    }
        ,
        this.update = function(t) {
        this.active && (this.xWiggle && (this.xWiggle *= Math.pow(.99, t)),
                        this.yWiggle && (this.yWiggle *= Math.pow(.99, t)),
                        this.turnSpeed && (this.dir += this.turnSpeed * t))
    }
}

        p.send(this.id, "8", Math.round(this.x), Math.round(this.y), i.volcanoDamagePerSecond, -1),
        this.timeSpentNearVolcano %= 1e3)),
            this.shameTimer > 0 && (this.shameTimer -= k,
                                    this.shameTimer <= 0 && (this.shameTimer = 0,
                                                             this.shameCount = 0)),
            v -= k,
            v <= 0) {
            const _ = (this.skin && this.skin.healthRegen ? this.skin.healthRegen : 0) + (this.tail && this.tail.healthRegen ? this.tail.healthRegen : 0);
            _ && this.changeHealth(_, this),
                this.dmgOverTime.dmg && (this.changeHealth(-this.dmgOverTime.dmg, this.dmgOverTime.doer),
                                         this.dmgOverTime.time -= 1,
                                         this.dmgOverTime.time <= 0 && (this.dmgOverTime.dmg = 0)),
                this.healCol && this.changeHealth(this.healCol, this),
                v = 1e3
        }
        if (!this.alive)
            return;
        if (this.slowMult < 1 && (this.slowMult += 8e-4 * k,
                                  this.slowMult > 1 && (this.slowMult = 1)),
            this.noMovTimer += k,
            (this.xVel || this.yVel) && (this.noMovTimer = 0),
            this.lockMove)
            this.xVel = 0,
                this.yVel = 0;
        else {
            let _ = (this.buildIndex >= 0 ? .5 : 1) * (c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].spdMult || 1) * (this.skin && this.skin.spdMult || 1) * (this.tail && this.tail.spdMult || 1) * (this.y <= i.snowBiomeTop ? this.skin && this.skin.coldM ? 1 : i.snowSpeed : 1) * this.slowMult;
            !this.zIndex && this.y >= i.mapScale / 2 - i.riverWidth / 2 && this.y <= i.mapScale / 2 + i.riverWidth / 2 && (this.skin && this.skin.watrImm ? (_ *= .75,
            this.xVel += i.waterCurrent * .4 * k) : (_ *= .33,
                                                     this.xVel += i.waterCurrent * k));
            let J = this.moveDir != null ? rt(this.moveDir) : 0
            , F = this.moveDir != null ? ot(this.moveDir) : 0;
            const z = Oc(J * J + F * F);
            z != 0 && (J /= z,
                       F /= z),
                J && (this.xVel += J * this.speed * _ * k),
                F && (this.yVel += F * this.speed * _ * k)
        }
        this.zIndex = 0,
            this.lockMove = !1,
            this.healCol = 0;
        let O;
        const V = s.getDistance(0, 0, this.xVel * k, this.yVel * k)
        , N = Math.min(4, Math.max(1, Math.round(V / 40)))
        , W = 1 / N;
        let P = {};
        for (var U = 0; U < N; ++U) {
            this.xVel && (this.x += this.xVel * k * W),
                this.yVel && (this.y += this.yVel * k * W),
                O = r.getGridArrays(this.x, this.y, this.scale);
            for (let _ = 0; _ < O.length; ++_) {
                for (let J = 0; J < O[_].length && !(O[_][J].active && !P[O[_][J].sid] && r.checkCollision(this, O[_][J], W) && (P[O[_][J].sid] = !0,
                                                                                                                                 !this.alive)); ++J)
                    ;
                if (!this.alive)
                    break
            }
            if (!this.alive)
                break
        }
        for (var L = o.indexOf(this), U = L + 1; U < o.length; ++U)
            o[U] != this && o[U].alive && r.checkCollision(this, o[U]);
        if (this.xVel && (this.xVel *= Os(i.playerDecel, k),
                          this.xVel <= .01 && this.xVel >= -.01 && (this.xVel = 0)),
            this.yVel && (this.yVel *= Os(i.playerDecel, k),
                          this.yVel <= .01 && this.yVel >= -.01 && (this.yVel = 0)),
            this.x - this.scale < 0 ? this.x = this.scale : this.x + this.scale > i.mapScale && (this.x = i.mapScale - this.scale),
            this.y - this.scale < 0 ? this.y = this.scale : this.y + this.scale > i.mapScale && (this.y = i.mapScale - this.scale),
            this.buildIndex < 0) {
            if (this.reloads[this.weaponIndex] > 0)
                this.reloads[this.weaponIndex] -= k,
                    this.gathering = this.mouseState;
            else if (this.gathering || this.autoGather) {
                let _ = !0;
                if (c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].gather != null)
                    this.gather(o);
                else if (c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].projectile != null && this.hasRes(c.weapons[this.weaponIndex], this.skin ? this.skin.projCost : 0)) {
                    this.useRes(c.weapons[this.weaponIndex], this.skin ? this.skin.projCost : 0),
                        this.noMovTimer = 0;
                    var L = c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].projectile;
                    const F = this.scale * 2
                    , z = this.skin && this.skin.aMlt ? this.skin.aMlt : 1;
                    c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].rec && (this.xVel -= c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].rec * rt(this.dir),
                                                        this.yVel -= c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].rec * ot(this.dir)),
                        n.addProjectile(this.x + F * rt(this.dir), this.y + F * ot(this.dir), this.dir, c.projectiles[L].range * z, c.projectiles[L].speed * z, L, this, null, this.zIndex)
                } else
                    _ = !1;
                this.gathering = this.mouseState,
                    _ && (this.reloads[this.weaponIndex] = c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].speed * (this.skin && this.skin.atkSpd || 1))
            }
        }
    }
        ,
        this.addWeaponXP = function(k) {
        this.weaponXP[this.weaponIndex] || (this.weaponXP[this.weaponIndex] = 0),
            this.weaponXP[this.weaponIndex] += k
    }
        ,
        this.earnXP = function(k) {
        this.age < i.maxAge && (this.XP += k,
                                this.XP >= this.maxXP ? (this.age < i.maxAge ? (this.age++,
                                                                                this.XP = 0,
                                                                                this.maxXP *= 1.2) : this.XP = this.maxXP,
                                                         this.upgradePoints++,
                                                         p.send(this.id, "U", this.upgradePoints, this.upgrAge),
                                                         p.send(this.id, "T", this.XP, s.fixTo(this.maxXP, 1), this.age)) : p.send(this.id, "T", this.XP))
    }
        ,
        this.changeHealth = function(k, T) {
        if (k > 0 && this.health >= this.maxHealth)
            return !1;
        k < 0 && this.skin && (k *= this.skin.dmgMult || 1),
            k < 0 && this.tail && (k *= this.tail.dmgMult || 1),
            k < 0 && (this.hitTime = Date.now()),
            this.health += k,
            this.health > this.maxHealth && (k -= this.health - this.maxHealth,
                                             this.health = this.maxHealth),
            this.health <= 0 && this.kill(T);
        for (let O = 0; O < o.length; ++O)
            this.sentTo[o[O].id] && p.send(o[O].id, "O", this.sid, this.health);
        return T && T.canSee(this) && !(T == this && k < 0) && p.send(T.id, "8", Math.round(this.x), Math.round(this.y), Math.round(-k), 1),
            !0
    }
        ,
        this.kill = function(k) {
        k && k.alive && (k.kills++,
                         k.skin && k.skin.goldSteal ? h(k, Math.round(this.points / 2)) : h(k, Math.round(this.age * 100 * (k.skin && k.skin.kScrM ? k.skin.kScrM : 1))),
                         p.send(k.id, "N", "kills", k.kills, 1)),
            this.alive = !1,
            p.send(this.id, "P"),
            m()
    }
        ,
        this.addResource = function(k, T, O) {
        !O && T > 0 && this.addWeaponXP(T),
            k == 3 ? h(this, T, !0) : (this[i.resourceTypes[k]] += T,
                                       p.send(this.id, "N", i.resourceTypes[k], this[i.resourceTypes[k]], 1))
    }
        ,
        this.changeItemCount = function(k, T) {
        this.itemCounts[k] = this.itemCounts[k] || 0,
            this.itemCounts[k] += T,
            p.send(this.id, "S", k, this.itemCounts[k])
    }
        ,
        this.buildItem = function(k) {
        const T = this.scale + k.scale + (k.placeOffset || 0)
        , O = this.x + T * rt(this.dir)
        , V = this.y + T * ot(this.dir);
        if (this.canBuild(k) && !(k.consume && this.skin && this.skin.noEat) && (k.consume || r.checkItemLocation(O, V, k.scale, .6, k.id, !1, this))) {
            let N = !1;
            if (k.consume) {
                if (this.hitTime) {
                    const W = Date.now() - this.hitTime;
                    this.hitTime = 0,
                        W <= 120 ? (this.shameCount++,
                                    this.shameCount >= 8 && (this.shameTimer = 3e4,
                                                             this.shameCount = 0)) : (this.shameCount -= 2,
                                                                                      this.shameCount <= 0 && (this.shameCount = 0))
                }
                this.shameTimer <= 0 && (N = k.consume(this))
            } else
                N = !0,
                    k.group.limit && this.changeItemCount(k.group.id, 1),
                    k.pps && (this.pps += k.pps),
                    r.add(r.objects.length, O, V, this.dir, k.scale, k.type, k, !1, this);
            N && (this.useRes(k),
                  this.buildIndex = -1)
        }
    }
        ,
        this.hasRes = function(k, T) {
        for (let O = 0; O < k.req.length; ) {
            if (this[k.req[O]] < Math.round(k.req[O + 1] * (T || 1)))
                return !1;
            O += 2
        }
        return !0
    }
        ,
        this.useRes = function(k, T) {
        if (!i.inSandbox)
            for (let O = 0; O < k.req.length; )
                this.addResource(i.resourceTypes.indexOf(k.req[O]), -Math.round(k.req[O + 1] * (T || 1))),
                    O += 2
    }
        ,
        this.canBuild = function(k) {
        const T = i.inSandbox ? k.group.sandboxLimit || Math.max(k.group.limit * 3, 99) : k.group.limit;
        return T && this.itemCounts[k.group.id] >= T ? !1 : i.inSandbox ? !0 : this.hasRes(k)
    }
        ,
        this.gather = function() {
        this.noMovTimer = 0,
            this.slowMult -= c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].hitSlow || .3,
            this.slowMult < 0 && (this.slowMult = 0);
        const k = i.fetchVariant(this)
        , T = k.poison
        , O = k.val
        , V = {};
        let N, W, P, U;
        const L = r.getGridArrays(this.x, this.y, c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].range);
        for (let J = 0; J < L.length; ++J)
            for (var _ = 0; _ < L[J].length; ++_)
                if (P = L[J][_],
                    P.active && !P.dontGather && !V[P.sid] && P.visibleToPlayer(this) && (N = s.getDistance(this.x, this.y, P.x, P.y) - P.scale,
                                                                                          N <= c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].range && (W = s.getDirection(P.x, P.y, this.x, this.y),
                                                                                                                                     s.getAngleDist(W, this.dir) <= i.gatherAngle))) {
                    if (V[P.sid] = 1,
                        P.health) {
                        if (P.changeHealth(-c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].dmg * O * (c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].sDmg || 1) * (this.skin && this.skin.bDmg ? this.skin.bDmg : 1), this)) {
                            for (let F = 0; F < P.req.length; )
                                this.addResource(i.resourceTypes.indexOf(P.req[F]), P.req[F + 1]),
                                    F += 2;
                            r.disableObj(P)
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (P.name === "volcano")
                            this.hitVolcano(c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].gather);
                        else {
                            this.earnXP(4 * c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].gather);
                            const F = c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].gather + (P.type == 3 ? 4 : 0);
                            this.addResource(P.type, F)
                        }
                        this.skin && this.skin.extraGold && this.addResource(3, 1)
                    }
                    U = !0,
                        r.hitObj(P, W)
                }
        for (var _ = 0; _ < o.length + l.length; ++_)
            if (P = o[_] || l[_ - o.length],
                P != this && P.alive && !(P.team && P.team == this.team) && (N = s.getDistance(this.x, this.y, P.x, P.y) - P.scale * 1.8,
                                                                             N <= c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].range && (W = s.getDirection(P.x, P.y, this.x, this.y),
                                                                                                                        s.getAngleDist(W, this.dir) <= i.gatherAngle))) {
                let F = c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].steal;
                F && P.addResource && (F = Math.min(P.points || 0, F),
                                       this.addResource(3, F),
                                       P.addResource(3, -F));
                let z = O;
                P.weaponIndex != null && c.weapons[P.weaponIndex].shield && s.getAngleDist(W + Math.PI, P.dir) <= i.shieldAngle && (z = c.weapons[P.weaponIndex].shield);
                const G = c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].dmg
                , X = G * (this.skin && this.skin.dmgMultO ? this.skin.dmgMultO : 1) * (this.tail && this.tail.dmgMultO ? this.tail.dmgMultO : 1)
                , te = .3 * (P.weightM || 1) + (c.weapons[this.weaponIndex].knock || 0);
                P.xVel += te * rt(W),
                    P.yVel += te * ot(W),
                    this.skin && this.skin.healD && this.changeHealth(X * z * this.skin.healD, this),
                    this.tail && this.tail.healD && this.changeHealth(X * z * this.tail.healD, this),
                    P.skin && P.skin.dmg && this.changeHealth(-G * P.skin.dmg, P),
                    P.tail && P.tail.dmg && this.changeHealth(-G * P.tail.dmg, P),
                    P.dmgOverTime && this.skin && this.skin.poisonDmg && !(P.skin && P.skin.poisonRes) && (P.dmgOverTime.dmg = this.skin.poisonDmg,
                                                                                                           P.dmgOverTime.time = this.skin.poisonTime || 1,
                                                                                                           P.dmgOverTime.doer = this),
                    P.dmgOverTime && T && !(P.skin && P.skin.poisonRes) && (P.dmgOverTime.dmg = 5,
                                                                            P.dmgOverTime.time = 5,
                                                                            P.dmgOverTime.doer = this),
                    P.skin && P.skin.dmgK && (this.xVel -= P.skin.dmgK * rt(W),
                                              this.yVel -= P.skin.dmgK * ot(W)),
                    P.changeHealth(-X * z, this, this)
            }
        this.sendAnimation(U ? 1 : 0)
    }
        ,
        this.hitVolcano = function(k) {
        const T = 5 + Math.round(k / 3.5);
        this.addResource(2, T),
            this.addResource(3, T)
    }
        ,
        this.sendAnimation = function(k) {
        for (let T = 0; T < o.length; ++T)
            this.sentTo[o[T].id] && this.canSee(o[T]) && p.send(o[T].id, "K", this.sid, k ? 1 : 0, this.weaponIndex)
    }
    ;
    let x = 0
    , A = 0;
    // player show dir
    this.animate = function(e) {
        let k = 13;
        this.animTime > 0 && (this.animTime -= k,
                              this.animTime <= 0 ? (this.animTime = 0,
                                                    this.dirPlus = 0,
                                                    x = 0,
                                                    A = 0) : A == 0 ? (x += ((2*e)/this.animSpeed),//(k / (this.animSpeed * i.hitReturnRatio)),
                                                                       this.dirPlus = s.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.min(1, x)),
                                                                       x >= 1 && (x = 1,
                                                                                  A = 1)) : (x -= ((2*e)/this.animSpeed),//(k / (this.animSpeed * (1 - i.hitReturnRatio))),
                                                                                             this.dirPlus = s.lerp(0, this.targetAngle, Math.max(0, x))))
    }
        ,
        this.startAnim = function(k, T) {
        this.animTime = this.animSpeed = c.weapons[T].speed,
            this.targetAngle = k ? -i.hitAngle : -Math.PI,
            x = 0,
            A = 0
    }
        ,
        this.canSee = function(k) {
        if (!k || k.skin && k.skin.invisTimer && k.noMovTimer >= k.skin.invisTimer)
            return !1;
        const T = Ds(k.x - this.x) - k.scale
        , O = Ds(k.y - this.y) - k.scale;
        return T <= i.maxScreenWidth / 2 * 1.3 && O <= i.maxScreenHeight / 2 * 1.3
    }
}

he.prototype.computeDirection = function(e) {

    if (t > i && t < i * 3 && !e.lockX ? n = "up" : t > -i && t <= i && !e.lockY ? n = "left" : t > -i * 3 && t <= -i && !e.lockX ? n = "down" : e.lockY || (n = "right"),
        e.lockY || (t > -s && t < s ? r = "left" : r = "right"),
        e.lockX || (t > 0 ? o = "up" : o = "down"),
        e.force > this.options.threshold) {
        var l = {}, c;
        for (c in this.direction)
            this.direction.hasOwnProperty(c) && (l[c] = this.direction[c]);
        var a = {};

            x: r,
            y: o,
            angle: n
        },
            e.direction = this.direction;
        for (c in l)
            l[c] === this.direction[c] && (a[c] = !0);
        if (a.x && a.y && a.angle)
            return e;
        (!a.x || !a.y) && this.trigger("plain", e),
            a.x || this.trigger("plain:" + r, e),
            a.y || this.trigger("plain:" + o, e),
            a.angle || this.trigger("dir dir:" + n, e)
    } else
        this.resetDirection();
    return e
}

oe.prototype.processOnMove = function(e) {
    var t = this
    , i = t.options
    , s = t.manager.getIdentifier(e)
    , n = t.nipples.get(s)
    , r = t.manager.scroll;

        this.processOnEnd(e);
        return
    }

        console.error("Found zombie joystick with ID " + s),
            t.manager.removeIdentifier(s);
        return
    }
    if (i.dynamicPage) {
        var o = n.el.getBoundingClientRect();
        n.position = {
            x: r.x + o.left,
            y: r.y + o.top
        }
    }
    n.identifier = s;
    var l = n.options.size / 2
    , c = {
        x: e.pageX,
        y: e.pageY
    };
    i.lockX && (c.y = n.position.y),
        i.lockY && (c.x = n.position.x);
    var a = hi(c, n.position), u = gh(c, n.position), p = On(u), h = a / l, m = {
        distance: a,
        position: c
    }, w, v;
    if (n.options.shape === "circle" ? (w = Math.min(a, l),
                                        v = yh(n.position, w, u)) : (v = bh(c, n.position, l),
                                                                     w = hi(v, n.position)),
        i.follow) {
        if (a > l) {
            let T = c.x - v.x
            , O = c.y - v.y;

                n.position.y += O,
                n.el.style.top = n.position.y - (t.box.top + r.y) + "px",
                n.el.style.left = n.position.x - (t.box.left + r.x) + "px",
                a = hi(c, n.position)
        }
    } else
        c = v,
            a = w;

    , A = c.y - n.position.y;

        x,
        y: A
    },
        i.dataOnly || (n.ui.front.style.transform = "translate(" + x + "px," + A + "px)");

        identifier: n.identifier,
        position: c,

        pressure: e.force || e.pressure || e.webkitForce || 0,
        distance: a,
        angle: {
            radian: p,
            degree: u
        },
        vector: {
            x: x / l,
            y: -A / l
        },
        raw: m,
        instance: n,
        lockX: i.lockX,
        lockY: i.lockY
    };
    k = n.computeDirection(k),
        k.angle = {
        radian: On(180 - u),
        degree: 180 - u
    },

}

, ho = Math.PI
, Je = ho * 2;
Math.lerpAngle = function(e, t, i) {
    Math.abs(t - e) > ho && (e > t ? t += Je : e += Je);
    const n = t + (e - t) * i;
    return n >= 0 && n <= Je ? n : n % Je
}

CanvasRenderingContext2D.prototype.roundRect = function(e, t, i, s, n) {
    return i < 2 * n && (n = i / 2),
        s < 2 * n && (n = s / 2),
        n < 0 && (n = 0),
        this.beginPath(),
        this.moveTo(e + n, t),
        this.arcTo(e + i, t, e + i, t + s, n),
        this.arcTo(e + i, t + s, e, t + s, n),
        this.arcTo(e, t + s, e, t, n),
        this.arcTo(e, t, e + i, t, n),
        this.closePath(),
        this
}

}
const wr = {};

        const r = R.projectiles[i.indx].src;

              o.onload = function() {

        }

    } else
        i.indx == 1 && (s.fillStyle = "#939393",
                        Q(e, t, i.scale, s))
}

        M.drawImage(Me.lava, Me.x - n - e, Me.y - n - t, n * 2, n * 2)
}

function Ro(e, t, i, s) {

        !De) {

            this.isLoaded = !0,
                this.onload = null
        }
            ,
            r.src = "./img/hats/hat_" + e + ".png",
            xr[e] = r,
            De = r
    }

    if (!n) {
        for (let r = 0; r < Xt.length; ++r)
            if (Xt[r].id == e) {
                n = Xt[r];
                break
            }
        br[e] = n
    }
    De.isLoaded && t.drawImage(De, -n.scale / 2, -n.scale / 2, n.scale, n.scale),
        !i && n.topSprite && (t.save(),
                              t.rotate(s.skinRot),
                              Ro(e + "_top", t, n, s),
                              t.restore())
}

    e.closePath()
}

function vs(e, t) {

    if (!i || t) {
        const c = document.createElement("canvas");
        c.width = c.height = e.scale * 2.5 + We + (R.list[e.id].spritePadding || 0);
        const a = c.getContext("2d");
        if (a.translate(c.width / 2, c.height / 2),
            a.rotate(t ? 0 : Math.PI / 2),
            a.strokeStyle = Zt,
            a.lineWidth = We * (t ? c.width / 81 : 1),
            e.name == "apple") {
            a.fillStyle = "#c15555",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#89a54c";
            const u = -(Math.PI / 2);
            Uf(e.scale * Math.cos(u), e.scale * Math.sin(u), 25, u + Math.PI / 2, a)
        } else if (e.name == "cookie") {
            a.fillStyle = "#cca861",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#937c4b";
            for (var s = 4, n = Je / s, r, o = 0; o < s; ++o)
                r = C.randInt(e.scale / 2.5, e.scale / 1.7),
                    Q(r * Math.cos(n * o), r * Math.sin(n * o), C.randInt(4, 5), a, !0)
        } else if (e.name == "cheese") {
            a.fillStyle = "#f4f3ac",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#c3c28b";
            for (var s = 4, n = Je / s, r, o = 0; o < s; ++o)
                r = C.randInt(e.scale / 2.5, e.scale / 1.7),
                    Q(r * Math.cos(n * o), r * Math.sin(n * o), C.randInt(4, 5), a, !0)
        } else if (e.name == "wood wall" || e.name == "stone wall" || e.name == "castle wall") {
            a.fillStyle = e.name == "castle wall" ? "#83898e" : e.name == "wood wall" ? "#a5974c" : "#939393";
            const u = e.name == "castle wall" ? 4 : 3;
            Ie(a, u, e.scale * 1.1, e.scale * 1.1),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = e.name == "castle wall" ? "#9da4aa" : e.name == "wood wall" ? "#c9b758" : "#bcbcbc",
                Ie(a, u, e.scale * .65, e.scale * .65),
                a.fill()
        } else if (e.name == "spikes" || e.name == "greater spikes" || e.name == "poison spikes" || e.name == "spinning spikes") {
            a.fillStyle = e.name == "poison spikes" ? "#7b935d" : "#939393";
            var l = e.scale * .6;
            Ie(a, e.name == "spikes" ? 5 : 6, e.scale, l),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = "#a5974c",
                Q(0, 0, l, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#c9b758",
                Q(0, 0, l / 2, a, !0)
        } else if (e.name == "windmill" || e.name == "faster windmill" || e.name == "power mill")
            a.fillStyle = "#a5974c",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#c9b758",
                In(0, 0, e.scale * 1.5, 29, 4, a),
                a.fillStyle = "#a5974c",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale * .5, a);
        else if (e.name == "mine")
            a.fillStyle = "#939393",
                Ie(a, 3, e.scale, e.scale),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = "#bcbcbc",
                Ie(a, 3, e.scale * .55, e.scale * .65),
                a.fill();
        else if (e.name == "sapling")
            for (var o = 0; o < 2; ++o) {
                var l = e.scale * (o ? .5 : 1);
                Ie(a, 7, l, l * .7),
                    a.fillStyle = o ? "#b4db62" : "#9ebf57",
                    a.fill(),
                    o || a.stroke()
            }
        else if (e.name == "pit trap")
            a.fillStyle = "#a5974c",
                Ie(a, 3, e.scale * 1.1, e.scale * 1.1),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = Zt,
                Ie(a, 3, e.scale * .65, e.scale * .65),
                a.fill();
        else if (e.name == "boost pad")
            a.fillStyle = "#7e7f82",
                wt(0, 0, e.scale * 2, e.scale * 2, a),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = "#dbd97d",
                Nf(e.scale * 1, a);
        else if (e.name == "turret") {
            a.fillStyle = "#a5974c",
                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke(),
                a.fillStyle = "#939393";
            const u = 50;
            wt(0, -u / 2, e.scale * .9, u, a),
                Q(0, 0, e.scale * .6, a),
                a.fill(),
                a.stroke()
        } else if (e.name == "platform") {
            a.fillStyle = "#cebd5f";
            const u = 4
            , p = e.scale * 2
            , h = p / u;
            let m = -(e.scale / 2);
            for (var o = 0; o < u; ++o)
                wt(m - h / 2, 0, h, e.scale * 2, a),
                    a.fill(),
                    a.stroke(),
                    m += p / u
        } else
            e.name == "healing pad" ? (a.fillStyle = "#7e7f82",
                                       wt(0, 0, e.scale * 2, e.scale * 2, a),
                                       a.fill(),
                                       a.stroke(),
                                       a.fillStyle = "#db6e6e",
                                       In(0, 0, e.scale * .65, 20, 4, a, !0)) : e.name == "spawn pad" ? (a.fillStyle = "#7e7f82",
                                                                                                         wt(0, 0, e.scale * 2, e.scale * 2, a),
                                                                                                         a.fill(),
                                                                                                         a.stroke(),
                                                                                                         a.fillStyle = "#71aad6",
                                                                                                         Q(0, 0, e.scale * .6, a)) : e.name == "blocker" ? (a.fillStyle = "#7e7f82",
            Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
            a.fill(),
            a.stroke(),
            a.rotate(Math.PI / 4),
            a.fillStyle = "#db6e6e",
            In(0, 0, e.scale * .65, 20, 4, a, !0)) : e.name == "teleporter" && (a.fillStyle = "#7e7f82",
                                                                                Q(0, 0, e.scale, a),
                                                                                a.fill(),
                                                                                a.stroke(),
                                                                                a.rotate(Math.PI / 4),
                                                                                a.fillStyle = "#d76edb",
                                                                                Q(0, 0, e.scale * .5, a, !0));
        i = c,
            t || (Pr[e.id] = i)
    }
    return i
}
function Uf(e, t, i, s, n) {
    const r = e + i * Math.cos(s)
    , o = t + i * Math.sin(s)
    , l = i * .4;
    n.moveTo(e, t),
        n.beginPath(),
        n.quadraticCurveTo((e + r) / 2 + l * Math.cos(s + Math.PI / 2), (t + o) / 2 + l * Math.sin(s + Math.PI / 2), r, o),
        n.quadraticCurveTo((e + r) / 2 - l * Math.cos(s + Math.PI / 2), (t + o) / 2 - l * Math.sin(s + Math.PI / 2), e, t),
        n.closePath(),
        n.fill(),
        n.stroke()
}
function Q(e, t, i, s, n, r) {
    s = s || M,
        s.beginPath(),
        s.arc(e, t, i, 0, 2 * Math.PI),
        r || s.fill(),
        n || s.stroke()
}
function Ie(e, t, i, s) {
    let n = Math.PI / 2 * 3, r, o;
    const l = Math.PI / t;
    e.beginPath(),
        e.moveTo(0, -i);
    for (let c = 0; c < t; c++)
        r = Math.cos(n) * i,
            o = Math.sin(n) * i,
            e.lineTo(r, o),
            n += l,
            r = Math.cos(n) * s,
            o = Math.sin(n) * s,
            e.lineTo(r, o),
            n += l;
    e.lineTo(0, -i),
        e.closePath()
}
function wt(e, t, i, s, n, r) {
    n.fillRect(e - i / 2, t - s / 2, i, s),
        r || n.strokeRect(e - i / 2, t - s / 2, i, s)
}
function In(e, t, i, s, n, r, o) {
    r.save(),
        r.translate(e, t),
        n = Math.ceil(n / 2);
    for (let l = 0; l < n; l++)
        wt(0, 0, i * 2, s, r, o),
            r.rotate(Math.PI / n);
    r.restore()
}
function Lf(e, t, i, s) {
    let n = Math.PI / 2 * 3;
    const r = Math.PI / t;
    let o;
    e.beginPath(),
        e.moveTo(0, -s);
    for (let l = 0; l < t; l++)
        o = C.randInt(i + .9, i * 1.2),
            e.quadraticCurveTo(Math.cos(n + r) * o, Math.sin(n + r) * o, Math.cos(n + r * 2) * s, Math.sin(n + r * 2) * s),
            n += r * 2;
    e.lineTo(0, -s),
        e.closePath()
}
function Nf(e, t) {
    t = t || M;
    const i = e * (Math.sqrt(3) / 2);
    t.beginPath(),
        t.moveTo(0, -i / 2),
        t.lineTo(-e / 2, i / 2),
        t.lineTo(e / 2, i / 2),
        t.lineTo(0, -i / 2),
        t.fill(),
        t.closePath()
}

let DAMAGE = 0, reSyncBull =false;
function iu(sid, value) {
    y = _i(sid);
    if (y) {
        let health = y.health;
        y.health = value;
        if (health < y.health) {
            if (y.hitTime) {
                let timeSinceHit = Date.now() - y.hitTime;
                let tmpShame = y.shameCount;
                y.hitTime = 0;
                if (timeSinceHit < 120) {
                    y.shameCount += 1;
                    if (y.shameCount > y.maxShame) {
                        y.maxShame = y.shameCount;
                    }
                    if (y.shameCount >= y.maxShame) {
                        y.addmaxShameTime = Date.now();
                    }

                    if (y.maxShame > 7) {
                        y.maxShame = 0;
                    }
                } else {
                    y.shameCount = Math.max(0, y.shameCount - 2);
                }
            }
        } else if (health > y.health) {
            y.hitTime = Date.now();
            y.hitted = true;
            y.damaged = true;
            let damage = health - y.health;
            if(y==E){
                setTimeout(()=>{
                    heal();
                    heal();
                    heal();
                },120);
                //     ShowText(y.x, y.y, damage, -1);
            }
            DAMAGE = damage;
            if (y.skinIndex == 7 && (damage == 5 || (y.tailIndex == 13 && damage == 2))) {
                //     y.bTick = ticks.tick;
                if (y == E) {
                    reSyncBull = false;
                }
            }
            //                               console.log(damage);
        }
    }
}

function heal(){
    if(E.food >= (E.items[0] === 0 ? 10 : E.items[0] === 1 ? 15 : 25) && E.health < 100 && E.skinIndex != 45){
        let heal = E.items[0] == 0 ? 20 : E.items[0] == 1 ? 40 : 30;
        let amount = (100 - E.health) / heal;
        for(let i = 0; i < amount; i++) {
            place(0, ks());
        }
    }

}let inSandbox = window.location.host.includes("sandbox");

function place(id, angle = Math.atan2(wo - gt / 2, yo - mt / 2)){
    try {
        var item = R.list[E.items[id]];
        if (E.itemCounts[item.group.id] == undefined ? true : E.itemCounts[item.group.id] < (inSandbox ? item.group.sandboxLimit ? item.group.sandboxLimit : 99 : item.group.limit ? item.group.limit : 99)) {
            Yt(E.items[id]);
            ee.send("d", 1, angle);
            Yt(E.weaponIndex, true);
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
function checkPlace(id, radian = Math.atan2(wo - gt / 2, yo - mt / 2)) {
    try {
        var item = R.list[E.items[id]];
        var tmpS = E.scale + item.scale + (item.placeOffset || 0);
        var tmpX = E.x2 + tmpS * Math.cos(radian);
        var tmpY = E.y2 + tmpS * Math.sin(radian);
        if (ee.sendCount < 100 && ue.checkItemLocation(tmpX, tmpY, item.scale, 0.6, item.id, false, E)) {
            if (E.itemCounts[item.group.id] == undefined ? true : E.itemCounts[item.group.id] < (inSandbox ? item.group.sandboxLimit ? item.group.sandboxLimit : 99 : item.group.limit ? item.group.limit : 99)) {
                place(id, radian);
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
let placelist = [];
function holdPlace(id, radian = Math.atan2(wo - gt / 2, yo - mt / 2)) {
    try {
        var item = R.list[E.items[id]];
        var tmpS = E.scale + item.scale + (item.placeOffset || 0);
        var tmpX = E.x2 + tmpS * Math.cos(radian);
        var tmpY = E.y2 + tmpS * Math.sin(radian);
        let canplace = true;
        for(let count = 0; count < placelist.length; count++){
            let DetectAngle = Math.hypot(item.scale, item.scale);
            if(radian + toRad(DetectAngle) > placelist[count][4] && radian - toRad(DetectAngle) < placelist[count][4]){
                canplace = false;
            }
        }
        if (ee.sendCount < 97 && canplace && ue.checkItemLocation(tmpX, tmpY, item.scale, 0.6, item.id, false, E)) {
            if (E.itemCounts[item.group.id] == undefined ? true : E.itemCounts[item.group.id] < (inSandbox ? item.group.sandboxLimit ? item.group.sandboxLimit : 99 : item.group.limit ? item.group.limit : 99)) {
                place(id, radian);
                placelist.push([tmpX, tmpY, tmpS, id, radian]);
                setTimeout(()=>{
                    placelist.shift();
                },parseInt(getID("placespeed").value));
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
function dist(tmp1, tmp2, type1, type2) {
    let a = {
        x: type1 == 0 ? tmp1.x : type1 == 1 ? tmp1.x1 : type1 == 2 ? tmp1.x2 : type1 == 3 && tmp1.x3,
        y: type1 == 0 ? tmp1.y : type1 == 1 ? tmp1.y1 : type1 == 2 ? tmp1.y2 : type1 == 3 && tmp1.y3,
    };
    let b = {
        x: type2 == 0 ? tmp2.x : type2 == 1 ? tmp2.x1 : type2 == 2 ? tmp2.x2 : type2 == 3 && tmp2.x3,
        y: type2 == 0 ? tmp2.y : type2 == 1 ? tmp2.y1 : type2 == 2 ? tmp2.y2 : type2 == 3 && tmp2.y3,
    };
    return Math.hypot(a.y - b.y, a.x - b.x);
}
function fixTo(n, v) {
    return parseFloat(n.toFixed(v));
}
function aim(tmp1, tmp2, type1, type2) {
    let tmpXY1 = {
        x: type1 == 0 ? tmp1.x : type1 == 1 ? tmp1.x1 : type1 == 2 ? tmp1.nextx : type1 == 3 && tmp1.x3,
        y: type1 == 0 ? tmp1.y : type1 == 1 ? tmp1.y1 : type1 == 2 ? tmp1.nexty : type1 == 3 && tmp1.y3,
    };
    let tmpXY2 = {
        x: type2 == 0 ? tmp2.x : type2 == 1 ? tmp2.x1 : type2 == 2 ? tmp2.nextx : type2 == 3 && tmp2.x3,
        y: type2 == 0 ? tmp2.y : type2 == 1 ? tmp2.y1 : type2 == 2 ? tmp2.nexty : type2 == 3 && tmp2.y3,
    };
    return Math.atan2(tmpXY1.y - tmpXY2.y, tmpXY1.x - tmpXY2.x);
}

function nu(e) {
    const t = Date.now();
    for (let i = 0; i < K.length; ++i) {
        if (K[i].visible) {
            K[i].forcePos = false;
            K[i].visible = false;
        }
    }
    for (let i = 0; i < e.length;) {
        y = _i(e[i]);
        if (y) {
            y.t1 = y.t2 === void 0 ? t : y.t2;
            y.t2 = t;
            y.x1 = y.x;
            y.y1 = y.y;
            y.x3 = y.x2;
            y.y3 = y.y2;
            y.x2 = e[i + 1];
            y.y2 = e[i + 2];
            y.speed = dist(y, y, 2, 3);
            if(E == y)speed = y.speed;
            y.dist = dist(y, E, 2, 2);
            y.aim = aim(y, E, 2, 2);
            y.d1 = y.d2 === void 0 ? e[i + 3] : y.d2;
            y.d2 = e[i + 3];
            y.dt = 0;
            y.buildIndex = e[i + 4];
            y.weaponIndex = e[i + 5];
            y.WeaponRange = R.weapons[y.weaponIndex].range;
            y.weaponVariant = e[i + 6];
            y.team = e[i + 7];
            y.isLeader = e[i + 8];
            y.skinIndex = e[i + 9];
            y.tailIndex = e[i + 10];
            y.iconIndex = e[i + 11];
            y.zIndex = e[i + 12];
            y.visible = true;
        }
        i += 13;
    }
}

        lr.hidden = !1
}

        window.setTimeout(e, 1e3 / 60)
    }
}();
